[Notes]: Mr. Hamilton is a 35yo M presenting with epigastric pain. The pain started 2 months ago but has been getting worse. He describes it as a gnawing, burning pain that rates 5/10 on the pain scale. Tums helped alleviate the pain initially but no longer work, the pain is not made worse with position changes, meals, or associated with any time of day. He denies any fever, chest pain, SOB, vomiting, diarrhea/constipation, or weight changes, but has had nausea and decreased appetite. He also endorses darkened stool but no melena or hematochezia
